   (function(){
        var queryParam = document.location.search;
        var referer = '';

        // query referer
        if (queryParam.length) {
            queryParam.substring(1).split('&').forEach(function(param) {
                if ('ref' === param.split('=')[0]) {
                    return referer = param.split('=')[1];
                }
            });
        }

        // natural referer
        if (!referer) {
            referer = window.document.referrer;
        }

        // add protocol
        if (referer && !new RegExp("https?://").exec(referer)) {
            referer = 'https://' + referer;
        }

        window.app = window.app || {};
        window.app.referer = referer;
    }())
  </script>

        <a href="/societe/3003763-20210321-bordeaux-jeune-anglaise-sauvagement-agressee-jeudi-dernier-cours-marne">

     <div class="lt-hoth-section-content">
      <div class="lt-hoth-row lt-hoth-row-3children">
